< review>
I've been to a few of them now, I think I can safely say that Sunright Tea Studio is definitely top tier in milk tea - this one was no exception! This one is in the middle of a indoor food plaza, so it might be a bit hard to find - just look for people waiting around for their drinks :D. Their milk tea and their Boca are both very good! Unfortunately I live in LA so I won't be able to visit this location as much, but it's good to know that Costa Mesa has an excellent milk tea spot if I'm in the area!</review>

<Date>1595754977708</Date><rate>4<//rate>< text>
(Current COVID-19 review)

So far I've been here quite a few times already. The drinks here are pretty consistent and they offer delivery and online ordering.  My constant go to drink is their Sunright Boba Milk Tea, the balance Of sweet and tea is excellent and when my gf came with me to try a fruit tea she said it was really good and their strawberry tea can rival Omomo. Lines here are usually short and workers here try to push drinks out fast, I do recommend 75% sugar since their milk tea drink can lean to be very sweet so 75% is good also ice level there is no need to adjust they don't put too much ice. I recommend this place, they do offer seating but it's closed currently due to COVID-19, and it's inside the OC mix next to Portolo Coffee. Happy boba drinking. They don't offer physical stamp cards but you can sign up for a rewards points on their iPad on the register and it'll link your card to your account, to later earn points for drinks!</text>

<user_id>118201532103612386053<//user_id><user_name>Christopher Karlsson< /user_name>< date>
1618418539826< /date>
<rating>4< /rating>< Text>
If the line is long (this happens even on cold days) and you haven't ordered ahead, be prepared to wait! The ice cream is a bit pricey, but the ingredients are high-quality, the flavors are plentiful and imaginative, and most importantly it is delicious!

If you like milkshakes, here's a tip: never get a regular milkshake from Handel's, and instead always get an "extra thick" shake. A regular milkshake is so thin, it's like flavored milk. An extra thick shake is like a regular shake from any other restaurant. Lastly, a pet peeve of mine is that they simply don't have drink carriers. If you are buying multiple milkshakes to go, you'll have to make multiple trips to your car, only carrying what you can safely hold in your hands. This is problematic if you have a toddler with you!<//Text>

<text>(Translated by Google) Wawona, located at the southern entrance to Yosemite, was originally an Indian settlement. In 1865, Galen Clark built a Clark Station in the name of his own name, and visitors to the Yosemite Valley could spend the night here. In 1864, the Mariposa Grove, consisting of the Yosemite Valley and the huge redwoods, was officially protected by the Yosemite Grant. Clark was nominated as the first director of Yosemite (guardian). In 1875, the Wawona Highway was opened to traffic, and the Washburn brothers acquired the land. They built the Wawona Lodge and are still open until now.
In Wawona, visitors can learn about the development of Yosemite and the people involved. Showcase historic pioneering houses and carriages at the Pioneer Yosemite History Center

(Original)

I had a very serious rodent issue (I was catching 2-4 mice a day) and they sent a third party exterminator to fix. <Rating>5</Rating><Review>This place is absolutely wonderful. I am from the east coast, but I plan on returning to Tulelake, CA just to eat here again. We came here twice during our visit to Lava Beds National Monument and both times were extremely enjoyable. The second night we came in five minutes before closing, fully expecting to be turned away and forced to eat our stale road snacks for dinner, but the friendly waitstaff welcomed us in and the chef even played the didgeridoo for us! Do not miss the desserts, either. They have the best pies. Even the photos on the walls are amazing. The chef is also a photographer and some of his pictures of the area are on display. I would highly recommend this restaurant to anyone!</Review><Response>None< /Response>< GmapID>

<review>There are two sites named Captain Jack's Stronghold. One is the restaurant on the highway and shown in the photos. The other is the historical site in the Lava Beds National Monument where Captain Jack and the Modocs held off the U.S. Cavalry for months and killed General Canby in 1873. It is an amazing redoubt, like a medieval castle with all the maze-like narrow pathways. It is no wonder the Modoc led the U.S. Cavalry on a wild goose chase for months, an episode that is long forgotten and supersed. The rough terrain is difficult on foot and even more so on horseback.om<//review>< Pictures>

<name>Virginia Massey< /name>< text>
I'm a Tulelake local and have been dining at Captain Jack's for many, many years.  The food is always great.  I usually find my way there a couple times a week for breakfast, lunch or dinner.  Service is excellent and friendly.  Love the homemade wheat bread served with dinner.  The only bad thing is that they are closed on Mondays and the whole month of January.  I'm usually going through withdrawal by the time February rolls around.  Definitely a great place to dine if you are visiting the Lava Beds or the Klamath Wildlife Refuge or just driving through the area.< /text>

<Review>After a long day at the caves, we were hoping for a satisfying dinner. There are very few options in TuleLake. We were not disappointed in Captain Jack's. I had the chicken, basil, artichoke pasta with excellent Alfredo sauce and julienne side veggies. A large serving, enough for two people. Primavera was also available. BF tried the fried oysters and loved them. The wheat bread and salad to start was great. We finished off with their lemon cheesecake with marionberry sauce. All around delicious meal in the midst of small town offerings. We had the restaurant all to ourselves (early dinner about 5pm). The hostess and cook were very friendly and chatted about the area. We are returning to Lava Beds in June and will definitely hit up this place again.< /Review>< pictures>

108685370139018629938< /userid>
< name>
Jay Keyes< /name>
<date>1577644717835</date>< rate>
5<//rate>
<text>The specialty of Tito's La Especial are "tacos al vapor," aka steamed tacos. This delicious Mexican street food is also known as "tacos de canasta" (basket tacos) because they're traditionally layered in a big basket and sold by street vendors, many of whom hawk them from their bikes.

Tito's "Carne Deshebrada Taco Al Vapor" is excellent. Aside from steamed double corn tortillas comprising each taco's "shell," the chile-steeped shredded beef inside is soft, luscious, and as juicy as you'd want any meat to be. You do want to eat these quickly, before the tortillas begin to stick to the wrappers they are served in. Despite the fact they traditionally would be drizzled in oil (to help preserve them) and served out of a basket over the course of a day, these tacos are best made-to-order. I would also recommend the "Papas Taco Al Vapor," consisting of seasoned potatoes in a ranchera sauce, a loose mash of creamy crushed potatoes and firmer chunks, all colored orange from the sauce.

The "Taco Dorado de Carne Deshebrada" served here is the complete opposite of the al vapor tacos, as the tortilla is instead a crunchy deep-fried shell that is stuffed with stewed beef, lettuce, chopped tomatoes, and shredded cheese. Tito's does a decent job with this style of taco, but you really should stick to the al vapor tacos here, which are indeed "especial."

Tito's La Especial's salsa roja is made of fire and miracles and I recommend it be used on everything you eat here.<//text><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOi1XyvPqLMkx0USiLiN0vgmzc5PMbnZW3Zy3ED=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipM_dAf952Lp4CXpcj4EwFcNvHGr-eCJOp448So4=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOAYocEnhdaptirVQEh4DqxQSODPVCsZxAcPPTM=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOmw0hZELb3PP9-z00K5BA2keJCNZX3kVLjolEJ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMw9TlAN-w6GJWCQ6JIhyyPOrIAANMX0txnpuUC=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOuAPcu6Jxdai3CiIrWyAHKoYOkR58VdEZOULRA=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNWXyYMOG3ZTjrLRaZPdPz2oMdCtwMyEkqf9Mw6=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /pics>< resp>
